***втыкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:втыкать.html>втыка́ть</a> (19794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тыкать.html>ты́кать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">týkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втыкать.html>втыка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vtykátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воткнуть.html>воткну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(in, into)</i>, to drive <i>(in, into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втыкать.html>втыка́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>кол</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtykátʹ</b> kol v zémlju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive a stake into the ground</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>вты<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:воткнуть.html>воткну́ть</a>.

***втягивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a> (9279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">втяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vtjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vtjágivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуть.html>втяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in, into, on, up</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to draw <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in, into, on, up</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to take in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjágivatʹ</b> vózdux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to draw/breathe/take in air</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жидкость.html>жи́дкость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjágivatʹ</b> žídkostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take in (suck up; absorb) liquid</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:коготь.html>ко́гти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjágivatʹ</b> kógti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to draw in its claws</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:втягивать.html>втя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёки</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>живо́т</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vtjágivatʹ</b> ščóki (živót)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to suck/pull in one's cheeks (stomach)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to draw <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">into</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to get involved <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втягиваться.html>втя́гиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vtjágivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуться.html>втяну́ться</a></b>)

<ol><li>to sag, to fall in</li>
<li>to get used, to get accustomed <i>(to)</i>, to feel at home <i>(with)</i>, to take <i>(to)</i>, to develop a liking <i>(for)</i>, to begin to enjoy

<li>to get mixed up <i>(in)</i>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втянуть.html>втяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vtjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:входить.html>входи́ть</a> (936)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:входить.html>входи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:войти.html>войти́</a></b>)

<li>to penetrate into</li>
<li>to be a part of</li></ol>

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:входить.html>входи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***вцепиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вцепиться.html>вцепи́ться</a> (3857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-цепи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-cepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепиться.html>вцепи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vcepítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепляться.html>вцепля́ться</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to seize, to grasp, to clutch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:злобный.html>зло́бно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепиться.html>вцепи́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná zlóbno <b>vcepílasʹ</b> jemú v vólosy.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She viciously seized him by the hair.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cling <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a sticky object</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to not let go, to get attached emotionally, to hate to be separated (from)</li>
<li>to bite <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of hunting dogs</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>вце<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пи́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:вцепляться.html>вцепля́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-цеп-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вцепляться.html>вцепля́ться</a> (28253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепиться.html>вцепи́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vcepítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепляться.html>вцепля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vcepljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вцепиться.html>вцепи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to seize, to snatch <i>(at)</i>, to catch hold <i>(of)</i>, to clutch <i>(at)</i>, to cling <i>(to)</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четверо.html>че́тверо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čétvero</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вчетверо.html>вче́тверо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">včétvero</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>in four rows or layers, in four
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сложить.html>сложи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>лист</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вчетверо.html>вче́тверо</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">složítʹ list <b>včétvero</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fold a sheet of paper <b>in four</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(by) four times <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in reference to a quantity, not to occurrences</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вчетверо.html>вче́тверо</a></b> ме́ньше</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>včétvero</b> ménʹše</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>four times</b> smaller</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезжать.html>въезжа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vʺjezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезд.html>въезд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vʺjezd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезд.html>въе́зда</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезд.html>въе́зды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезд.html>въе́здов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>entry, entrance <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act of entering, especially when using any means of transportation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>entry, entrance <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">doorway that provides a means of entering a building</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
